Part  VI—Section  2
Notiﬁ cation or Orders of interest to a section of the public 
issued by Heads of Departments, etc.
NOTIFICATIONS BY HEADS OF DEPARTMENTS, ETC.
DIRECTOR OF MUNICIPAL ADMINISTRATION
[DELIMITATION - DELIMITATION OF WARDS OF MUNICIPALITIES OF NINE NEWLY FORMED DISTRICT - 
AMENDMENT TO THE NOTIFICATION ISSUED.]
(Roc.No.575/2020/Election)
No.VI(2)/111(c)/2021.
WHEREAS in pursuance of the orders of the Hon’ble Supreme Court of India in I.A.No.182868 of 
2019 in Civil Appeal Nos.5467-5469 of 2017, dated the 6th December 2019, the Delimitation Commission 
constituted under the Tamil Nadu Delimitation Commission Act, 2017 (Tamil Nadu Act 23 of 2017), has 
submitted its recommendation on the territorial wards of Municipalities in the nine newly constituted districts 
to the Government, after having published the draft proposal for delimitation of the territorial wards of the 
Municipalities based on the last preceding census of which the relevant ﬁ gures have been published (2011 
census) for general information, by inviting and processing the objections / suggestions received thereon;
NOW, THEREFORE, in exercise of the powers conferred under sub-section (1) of section 43 of the 
Tamil Nadu District Municipalities Act, 1920 (Tamil Nadu Act V of 1920) and the powers delegated to the 
Commissioner of Municipal Administration in G.O.(Ms.)No.133, Municipal Administration and Water Supply 
Department, dated the 6th June 1996, published in Municipal Administration and Water Supply Department, 
Notiﬁ cation No. II/(2)/MW/1197 (c-2)/96 at page 1 in Part-II Section 2 of the Tamil Nadu Government Gazette, 
Extraordinary, dated the 6th June 1996 and based on the recommendations of the Delimitation Commission, 
the Director of Municipal Administration hereby, after consulting the Municipal Council concerned, makes the 
following amendments to Notiﬁ cation No.VI(2)/160(a-2)/2018 published at pages 1-465 in Part VI-Section 2 
of the Tamil Nadu Government Gazette, Extraordinary, dated the 14th December 2018:— 
 


2
